# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# OpenJDK G1 GC Garbage Collection Cycle Chain

## Your Task

Trace the G1 garbage collector's concurrent marking and mixed collection cycle in openjdk/jdk. Find C++ source files implementing: the G1ConcurrentMark start trigger, the SATB marking queue processing, the remembered set scanning, and the mixed collection region selection.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo domain.

- `sg-evals/jdk--742e735d` (openjdk/jdk)

Perfect! I've created a comprehensive analysis of the G1 garbage collector's concurrent marking and mixed collection cycle in openjdk/jdk. The answer includes:

## Summary of Findings

I've identified and documented all key components of the G1 GC concurrent marking and mixed collection cycle:

### 1. **G1ConcurrentMark Start Trigger**
- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1ConcurrentMark.cpp` - `post_concurrent_mark_start()` activates SATB marking queues
- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1ConcurrentMarkThread.cpp` - orchestrates concurrent phases

### 2. **SATB Marking Queue Processing**
- `src/hotspot/share/gc/shared/satbMarkQueue.hpp/cpp` - core SATB queue implementation
- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1SATBMarkQueueSet.cpp` - G1-specific queue set with `requires_marking()` filter that checks TAMS (Top At Mark Start)

### 3. **Remembered Set Scanning**
- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1RemSet.cpp` - `G1RemSetScanState` manages scanning progress
- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1HeapRegionRemSet.hpp` - per-region remembered sets
- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1CardSet.hpp/cpp` - efficient card set data structures
- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1RemSetTrackingPolicy.hpp` - determines which regions need rebuild

### 4. **Mixed Collection Region Selection**
- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1CollectionSetCandidates.hpp/cpp` - maintains list of candidate regions
- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1CollectionSetChooser.cpp` - `build()` selects regions by reclaimable bytes

The complete analysis with all 29 relevant files and detailed execution flow has been written to `/workspace/answer.json`.

Each heap region maintains a `G1HeapRegionRemSet` (src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1HeapRegionRemSet.hpp, line 42), which encapsulates remembered set information as a `G1CardSet` (src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1CardSet.hpp). The card set uses efficient memory structures managed by `G1CardSetMemory` (src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1CardSetMemory.hpp) to track inter-region references. During concurrent marking, remembered sets are rebuilt and maintain tracking state using `G1RemSetTrackingPolicy` (src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1RemSetTrackingPolicy.hpp), which determines which regions need remembered set updates.\\n\\n## 5. Regions are sorted by reclaimable bytes and then pruned according to `G1HeapWastePercent`. Selected regions transition the collector state to `in_mixed_phase()` (src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1CollectorState.hpp, line 100), enabling mixed collections that evacuate both young and selected old regions.\\n\\n## Summary of Key Implementation Files\\n\\n- **Concurrent Mark Control**: src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1ConcurrentMark.{hpp,cpp} and g1ConcurrentMarkThread.{hpp,cpp}\\n- **SATB Processing**: src/hotspot/share/gc/shared/satbMarkQueue.{hpp,cpp} and g1SATBMarkQueueSet.{hpp,cpp}\\n- **Marking Tasks**: src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1ConcurrentMark.hpp (G1CMTask) and g1OopClosures.{hpp,inline.hpp}\\n- **Remembered Set Infrastructure**: src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1RemSet.{hpp,cpp}, g1HeapRegionRemSet.{hpp,cpp}, g1CardSet.{hpp,cpp}, and g1CardSetMemory.{hpp,cpp}\\n- **Mixed Collection Selection**: src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1CollectionSetCandidates.{hpp,cpp}, g1CollectionSetChooser.{hpp,cpp}, and g1CollectionSet.{hpp,cpp}\\n\\nThe entire cycle is orchestrated by `G1Policy` (src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1Policy.{hpp,cpp}), which makes heuristic decisions about when to start marking, when to transition to mixed phase, and how aggressively to collect old regions based on heap occupancy and collection time targets.\"\n}\n",

Each heap region maintains a `G1HeapRegionRemSet` (src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1HeapRegionRemSet.hpp, line 42), which encapsulates remembered set information as a `G1CardSet` (src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1CardSet.hpp). The card set uses efficient memory structures managed by `G1CardSetMemory` (src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1CardSetMemory.hpp) to track inter-region references. During concurrent marking, remembered sets are rebuilt and maintain tracking state using `G1RemSetTrackingPolicy` (src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1RemSetTrackingPolicy.hpp), which determines which regions need remembered set updates.\\n\\n## 5. Mixed Collection Region Selection\\n\\nAfter concurrent marking completes, regions are selected for mixed collection through `G1CollectionSetCandidates` (src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1CollectionSetCandidates.hpp, line 205), which maintains a prioritized list of old generation regions for potential evacuation. The selection process is executed by `G1CollectionSetChooser::build()` (src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1CollectionSetChooser.cpp, line 262), which leverages `G1BuildCandidateRegionsTask` to identify high-value regions based on reclaimable garbage. Regions are sorted by reclaimable bytes and then pruned according to `G1HeapWastePercent`. Selected regions transition the collector state to `in_mixed_phase()` (src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1CollectorState.hpp, line 100), enabling mixed collections that evacuate both young and selected old regions.\\n\\n## Summary of Key Implementation Files\\n\\n- **Concurrent Mark Control**: src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1ConcurrentMark.{hpp,cpp} and g1ConcurrentMarkThread.{hpp,cpp}\\n- **SATB Processing**: src/hotspot/share/gc/shared/satbMarkQueue.{hpp,cpp} and g1SATBMarkQueueSet.{hpp,cpp}\\n- **Marking Tasks**: src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1ConcurrentMark.hpp (G1CMTask) and g1OopClosures.{hpp,inline.hpp}\\n- **Remembered Set Infrastructure**: src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1RemSet.{hpp,cpp}, g1HeapRegionRemSet.{hpp,cpp}, g1CardSet.{hpp,cpp}, and g1CardSetMemory.{hpp,cpp}\\n- **Mixed Collection Selection**: src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1CollectionSetCandidates.{hpp,cpp}, g1CollectionSetChooser.{hpp,cpp}, and g1CollectionSet.{hpp,cpp}\\n\\nThe entire cycle is orchestrated by `G1Policy` (src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1Policy.{hpp,cpp}), which makes heuristic decisions about when to start marking, when to transition to mixed phase, and how aggressively to collect old regions based on heap occupancy and collection time targets.\"\n}\n",
